  430: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  431: # Pipeline runner -- manages a single concurrent research run
  432: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  433: class PipelineRunner:
  434:     """Manages the lifecycle of a single research pipeline run.
  435: 
  436:     Only one run allowed at a time. The run executes in a background
  437:     asyncio task so the /api/research endpoint returns immediately.
  438:     """
  439: 
  440:     def __init__(self) -> None:
  441:         self._task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None
  442:         self._status = ResearchStatus()
  443:         self._lock = asyncio.Lock()
  444:         self._running: bool = False
  445:         self._tailer_watcher_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None
  446:         # D2: Live steering state
  447:         self._steer_directives: list[str] = []
  448:         self._steer_lock = asyncio.Lock()
  449: 
  450:     @property
  451:     def running(self) -> bool:
  452:         return self._task is not None and not self._task.done()
  453: 
  454:     @property
  455:     def status(self) -> ResearchStatus:
  456:         s = self._status.model_copy()
  457:         s.running = self.running
  458:         return s
  459: 
  460:     async def start(
  461:         self,
  462:         query: str,
  463:         depth: str,
  464:         application: str,
  465:         region: str,
  466:         document_ids: list[str] | None = None,
  467:         research_brief: str | None = None,
  468:     ) -> str:
  469:         """Start a new research run. Returns the vector_id."""
  470:         async with self._lock:
  471:             if self.running:
  472:                 raise RuntimeError("A research run is already in progress")
  473: 
  474:             # Validate depth against presets (strict -- no silent fallback)
  475:             if depth not in DEPTH_PRESETS:
  476:                 raise ValueError(
  477:                     f"Invalid depth '{depth}'. Must be one of: {list(DEPTH_PRESETS.keys())}"
  478:                 )
  479: 
  480:             # Generate vector_id from timestamp
  481:             ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y%m%dT%H%M%S")
  482:             query_hash = hashlib.sha256(query.encode()).hexdigest()[:6]
  483:             vector_id = f"WEB_{ts}_{query_hash}"
  484: 
  485:             max_iterations, max_minutes = DEPTH_PRESETS[depth]
  486: 
  487:             self._status = ResearchStatus(
  488:                 running=True,
  489:                 vector_id=vector_id,
  490:                 query=query,
  491:                 depth=depth,
  492:                 started_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
  493:                 status="starting",
  494:             )
  495: 
  496:             self._running = True
  497:             self._task = asyncio.create_task(
  498:                 self._run_pipeline(
  499:                     vector_id=vector_id,
  500:                     query=query,
  501:                     application=application,
  502:                     region=region,
  503:                     max_iterations=max_iterations,
  504:                     max_minutes=max_minutes,
  505:                     document_ids=document_ids or [],
  506:                     research_brief=research_brief,
  507:                 )
  508:             )
  509: 
  510:             return vector_id
  511: 
  512:     async def cancel(self) -> bool:
  513:         """Cancel the running research. Returns True if cancelled."""
  514:         async with self._lock:
  515:             if not self.running or self._task is None:
  516:                 return False
  517:             self._task.cancel()
  518:             self._status.status = "cancelled"
  519:             self._running = False
  520:             return True
  521: 
  522:     async def steer(self, directive: str) -> bool:
  523:         """Queue a steering directive for the running pipeline (D2)."""
  524:         async with self._steer_lock:
  525:             if not self.running:
  530: 
  531:     async def _run_pipeline(
  532:         self,
  533:         vector_id: str,
  534:         query: str,
  535:         application: str,
  536:         region: str,
  537:         max_iterations: int,
  538:         max_minutes: int,
  539:         document_ids: list[str] | None = None,
  540:         research_brief: str | None = None,
  541:     ) -> None:
  542:         """Execute the research pipeline in a background task."""
  543:         global _tailer, _trace_path
  544: 
  545:         try:
  546:             self._status.status = "running"
  547: 
  548:             # Import pipeline (deferred to avoid import-time side effects)
  549:             # BUG-B-102 R2e+R2g: v4 (pipeline-A-backed) is now the
  550:             # production default. v1/v2/v3 remain selectable via the
  551:             # explicit env flag for compatibility during migration.
  552:             # v4 enforces the 5-round pipeline-A hardening (strict_verify,
  553:             # corpus_approval, delimiter sanitization, unified manifest.status,
  554:             # evaluator gate, tier-balanced evidence selection).
  555:             graph_version = os.getenv("PG_GRAPH_VERSION", "v4")
  556:             if graph_version == "v4":
  557:                 from src.polaris_graph.graph_v4 import build_and_run_v4 as build_and_run
  558:             elif graph_version == "v3":
  559:                 from src.polaris_graph.graph_v3 import build_and_run_v3 as build_and_run
  560:             elif os.getenv("PG_V2_ENABLED", "0") == "1" or graph_version == "v2":
  561:                 from src.polaris_graph.graph_v2 import build_and_run
  562:             elif graph_version == "v1":
  563:                 from src.polaris_graph.graph import build_and_run
  564:             else:
  565:                 # Unknown version → safe default (v4, the hardened path).
  566:                 logger.warning(
  567:                     "Unknown PG_GRAPH_VERSION=%r; falling back to v4",
  568:                     graph_version,
  569:                 )
  570:                 from src.polaris_graph.graph_v4 import build_and_run_v4 as build_and_run
  571: 
  572:             # Point the trace tailer to the new trace file
  573:             new_trace_path = Path(PG_LIVE_TRACE_DIR) / f"pg_trace_{vector_id}.jsonl"
  574: 
  575:             # Clean up previous tailer watcher task if it exists
  576:             if self._tailer_watcher_task is not None and not self._tailer_watcher_task.done():
  577:                 self._tailer_watcher_task.cancel()
  578:                 try:
  579:                     await asyncio.shield(self._tailer_watcher_task)
  580:                 except (asyncio.CancelledError, Exception):
  581:                     pass
  582:                 self._tailer_watcher_task = None
  583: 
  584:             _trace_path = new_trace_path
  585:             _tailer = TraceTailer(new_trace_path)
  586:             # Start watching the new trace file
  587:             self._tailer_watcher_task = asyncio.create_task(_tailer.run_watcher())
  588: 
  589:             logger.info(
  590:                 "Starting research: vector_id=%s query=%r depth=%s/%d",
  591:                 vector_id,
  592:                 query[:80],
  593:                 max_iterations,
  594:                 max_minutes,
  595:             )
  596: 
  597:             # D2: Create steer_callback closure for live steering
  598:             def steer_callback() -> list[str]:
  599:                 """Drain pending steer directives (called from _evaluate node)."""
  600:                 directives = list(self._steer_directives)
  601:                 self._steer_directives.clear()
  602:                 return directives
  603: 
  604:             result = await build_and_run(
  605:                 vector_id=vector_id,
  606:                 query=query,
  607:                 application=application,
  608:                 region=region,
  609:                 max_iterations=max_iterations,
  610:                 max_execution_minutes=max_minutes,
  611:                 resume=False,
  612:                 enable_dashboard=False,  # No Rich terminal in server mode
  613:                 document_ids=document_ids or [],
  614:                 steer_callback=steer_callback,
  615:                 research_brief=research_brief,
  616:             )
  617: 
  618:             self._status.status = result.get("status", "completed")
  619:             result_path = f"outputs/polaris_graph/{vector_id}.json"
  620:             self._status.result_path = result_path
  621: 
  622:             logger.info(
  623:                 "Research completed: vector_id=%s status=%s",
  624:                 vector_id,
  625:                 self._status.status,

 1787: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1788: # Research pipeline endpoints
 1789: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1790: @app.post("/api/research")
 1791: async def start_research(request: Request, req: ResearchRequest):
 1792:     """Start a new research pipeline run.
 1793: 
 1794:     Accepts a research question and depth preset. Returns immediately
 1795:     with the vector_id; pipeline runs in background. Monitor progress
 1796:     via /api/events SSE stream.
 1797: 
 1798:     Rate-limited to 1 request per minute per client IP.
 1799:     """
 1800:     # --- Rate limiting ---
 1801:     if RATE_LIMIT_AVAILABLE and limiter is not None:
 1802:         # slowapi decorator applied via app.state.limiter
 1803:         # Manual check for non-decorator approach
 1804:         pass
 1805:     else:
 1806:         # Fallback in-memory rate limiter
 1807:         client_ip = request.client.host if request.client else "unknown"
 1808:         if not _fallback_limiter.check(client_ip):
 1809:             remaining = _fallback_limiter.seconds_remaining(client_ip)
 1810:             return JSONResponse(
 1811:                 {
 1812:                     "error": "Rate limit exceeded. Try again later.",
 1813:                     "retry_after_seconds": remaining,
 1814:                 },
 1815:                 status_code=429,
 1816:                 headers={"Retry-After": str(remaining)},
 1817:             )
 1818: 
 1819:     if _runner.running:
 1820:         return JSONResponse(
 1821:             {"error": "A research run is already in progress", "status": _runner.status.model_dump()},
 1822:             status_code=409,
 1823:         )
 1824: 
 1825:     # Strict depth validation (no silent fallback)
 1826:     if req.depth not in DEPTH_PRESETS:
 1827:         raise HTTPException(
 1828:             status_code=422,
 1829:             detail=f"Invalid depth '{req.depth}'. Must be one of: {list(DEPTH_PRESETS.keys())}",
 1830:         )
 1831: 
 1832:     try:
 1833:         vector_id = await _runner.start(
 1834:             query=req.query,
 1835:             depth=req.depth,
 1836:             application=req.application,
 1837:             region=req.region,
 1838:             document_ids=req.document_ids,
 1839:         )
 1840:     except ValueError as exc:
 1841:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail=str(exc))
 1842:     except Exception as exc:
 1843:         return JSONResponse(
 1844:             {"error": f"Failed to start research: {exc}"},
 1845:             status_code=500,
 1846:         )
 1847: 
 1848:     return JSONResponse({
 1849:         "vector_id": vector_id,
 1850:         "query": req.query,
 1851:         "depth": req.depth,
 1852:         "document_ids": req.document_ids,
 1853:         "message": "Research started. Monitor via /api/events SSE stream.",
 1854:     })
 1855: 
 1856: 
 1857: # Apply slowapi rate limit decorator if available
 1858: if RATE_LIMIT_AVAILABLE and limiter is not None:
 1859:     start_research = limiter.limit("1/minute")(start_research)

  143:             "content_preview": "GAC filtration for PFAS",

  145:             "content": "GAC filtration reduces PFAS to below 4 ppt per EPA guidelines. "
  146:                        "The system processes 2 MGD with EBCT of 10-20 minutes.",
  147:         }]
  148: 
  149:         # The analyzer reads uploaded_documents and injects evidence.
  150:         # We test the chunking logic directly.
  151:         uploaded_docs = state["uploaded_documents"]
  152:         evidence = []
  153:         chunk_size = 2000
  154:         max_chunks = 20
  155: 
  156:         for doc in uploaded_docs:
  157:             content = doc.get("content", "")
  158:             filename = doc.get("filename", "document")
  159:             doc_id = doc.get("doc_id", "unk")
  160: 
  161:             chunks = []
  162:             for i in range(0, len(content), chunk_size):
  163:                 chunk_text = content[i:i + chunk_size].strip()
  164:                 if len(chunk_text) >= 50:
  165:                     chunks.append({"text": chunk_text, "chunk_id": f"chunk_{i // chunk_size}"})
  166:             chunks = chunks[:max_chunks]
  167: 
  168:             for chunk in chunks:
  169:                 ev_id = f"ev_doc_{doc_id}_{chunk['chunk_id']}"
  170:                 evidence.append({
  171:                     "id": ev_id,
  172:                     "claim": chunk["text"][:500],
  173:                     "source_url": f"uploaded://{filename}",
  174:                     "source_title": filename,
  175:                     "tier": "gold",
  176:                     "source_type": "uploaded_document",
  177:                     "relevance": 0.95,
  178:                     "authority": 1.0,
  179:                     "perspective": "Primary Source",
  180:                     "direct_quote": chunk["text"],
  181:                 })

  183:         assert len(evidence) == 1
  184:         assert evidence[0]["id"] == "ev_doc_abc123_chunk_0"
  185:         assert evidence[0]["tier"] == "gold"
  186:         assert evidence[0]["source_type"] == "uploaded_document"
  187:         assert "GAC filtration" in evidence[0]["direct_quote"]
  188:         assert evidence[0]["source_url"] == "uploaded://contract.txt"
  189: 
  190:     def test_large_document_chunked_correctly(self):
  191:         """Documents larger than chunk_size are split into multiple evidence pieces."""
  192:         large_content = "X" * 5000  # 5000 chars > 2000 chunk_size
  193:         uploaded_docs = [{
  194:             "doc_id": "big_doc",
  195:             "filename": "large.txt",
  196:             "content": large_content,
  197:         }]
  198: 
  199:         evidence = []
  200:         chunk_size = 2000
  201:         max_chunks = 20
  202: 
  203:         for doc in uploaded_docs:
  204:             content = doc.get("content", "")
  205:             doc_id = doc.get("doc_id", "unk")
  206:             chunks = []
  207:             for i in range(0, len(content), chunk_size):
  208:                 chunk_text = content[i:i + chunk_size].strip()
  209:                 if len(chunk_text) >= 50:
  210:                     chunks.append({"text": chunk_text, "chunk_id": f"chunk_{i // chunk_size}"})
  211:             for chunk in chunks[:max_chunks]:
  212:                 evidence.append({"id": f"ev_doc_{doc_id}_{chunk['chunk_id']}"})
  213: 
  214:         assert len(evidence) == 3  # 5000 / 2000 = 2.5 → 3 chunks

  647: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  648: # CampaignManager: manages multi-query research campaigns
  649: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  650: class CampaignManager:
  651:     """Manages campaign lifecycle and sequential query execution.
  652: 
  653:     Campaigns queue multiple research queries and execute them one at a time
  654:     through the existing PipelineRunner. Supports snowball memory -- passing
  655:     summaries from completed queries as context to subsequent queries.
  656: 
  657:     Thread-safety: relies on asyncio single-threaded event loop.
  658:     Data persisted to SQLite via campaign_store (Sprint 1, Task 1A.2).
  659:     Falls back to in-memory only if campaign_store is unavailable.
  660:     """
  661: 
  662:     def __init__(self, runner: PipelineRunner) -> None:
  663:         self._campaigns: dict[str, CampaignData] = {}
  664:         self._runner = runner
  665:         self._active_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None
  666:         self._active_campaign_id: Optional[str] = None
  667: 
  668:     async def load_persisted_campaigns(self) -> None:
  669:         """Load campaigns from SQLite on startup (Sprint 1, Task 1A.2)."""
  670:         if not _CAMPAIGN_STORE_AVAILABLE or _db_list_campaigns is None:
  671:             logger.debug("Campaign store not available, skipping load")
  672:             return
  673:         try:
  674:             rows = await _db_list_campaigns()
  675:             for row in rows:
  676:                 cid = row.get("campaign_id", "")
  677:                 if not cid or cid in self._campaigns:
  678:                     continue
  679:                 queries_data = row.get("queries_json", [])
  680:                 queries = []
  681:                 for qd in (queries_data if isinstance(queries_data, list) else []):
  682:                     if isinstance(qd, dict):
  683:                         queries.append(CampaignQueryStatus(
  684:                             query=qd.get("query", ""),
  685:                             status=qd.get("status", "queued"),

  688:                             started_at=qd.get("started_at"),

  691:                             application=qd.get("application"),
  692:                             region=qd.get("region"),
  693:                         ))
  694:                 meta = row.get("metadata_json", {})
  695:                 if not isinstance(meta, dict):
  696:                     meta = {}

"""
POLARIS - Production-Grade Research Pipeline

FIX 120: Load environment variables at package initialization.
This ensures API keys are available before any module imports them.
"""
import os
from pathlib import Path

# Load .env file at package import time
from dotenv import load_dotenv

# Find the project root (parent of src/)
_PROJECT_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
_ENV_FILE = _PROJECT_ROOT / ".env"

if _ENV_FILE.exists():
    # LOOPBACK-FIX: override=False so pre-set os.environ values (from test
    # harnesses, CI configs, loopback scripts) win over .env defaults.
    # Was override=True which silently clobbered programmatic overrides.
    load_dotenv(_ENV_FILE, override=False)
"""
polaris graph — clean-room research pipeline.

Uses Qwen 3.5 Plus via OpenRouter for all LLM calls.
Reuses battle-tested search/fetch infrastructure from src/tools/.
"""

__all__ = [
    "run_research",
]


async def run_research(
    vector_id: str,
    query: str,
    application: str,
    region: str,
    stage: int = 1,
    max_iterations: int = 3,
    max_execution_minutes: int = 30,
):
    """Entry point for polaris graph research pipeline.

    Routes to v3/v2/v1 based on PG_GRAPH_VERSION env var.
    """
    import os
    graph_version = os.getenv("PG_GRAPH_VERSION", "v1")
    if graph_version == "v3":
        from src.polaris_graph.graph_v3 import build_and_run_v3 as build_and_run
    else:
        from src.polaris_graph.graph import build_and_run

    return await build_and_run(
        vector_id=vector_id,
        query=query,
        application=application,
        region=region,
        stage=stage,
        max_iterations=max_iterations,
        max_execution_minutes=max_execution_minutes,
    )

codex
The one meaningful concern I see is an error-surface mismatch: all-invalid document IDs fail before v4’s `run_one_query` exception adapter, so the live runner marks the task failed without a v4 UI JSON artifact. Given the brief explicitly requires fail-loud `RuntimeError` for all-failed documents, I’m treating that as residual P2 rather than a P1 blocker.
